style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Revenue in Q3 grew 15% (21% on a foreign exchange (F&#47;X) neutral basis</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">), 1% higher than our beginning of quarter forecast. ARM</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">2</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> was flat year over year and up 5% on a F&#47;X neutral basis</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">3</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">. Regional highlights include&#58;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;padding-left:12.53pt">UCAN, our most mature market, saw a 16% year over year increase in revenue, driven by 10% and 5% growth in average paid memberships and ARM, respectively.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;padding-left:12.53pt">Revenue in EMEA grew 16% year over year, consistent with the increase in average paid memberships.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;padding-left:12.53pt">We&#8217;re improving our product&#47;market fit in APAC and had a strong local content slate in Japan, Korea, Thailand and India in Q3. As a result, our revenue growth rate in APAC (+19% year over year) led all regions.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;padding-left:12.53pt">LATAM revenue rose 9% year over year. Paid net adds of -0.1M was due to recent price changes and a softer content slate. However, membership growth has rebounded nicely early in Q4&#8217;24.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Q3&#8217;24 operating income increased 52% year over year to $2.9B, while operating margin of 30% improved seven percentage points vs. the year ago quarter. This was above our guidance forecast due to slightly higher revenue and the timing of spending. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">EPS amounted to $5.40 vs. $3.73 (+45% year over year) and included a $91M loss from F&#47;X , predominantly related to our Euro denominated debt remeasurement (net of hedging impacts), which is recognized below operating income in &#8220;interest and other income&#8221;.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Forecast</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">As a reminder, the quarterly guidance we provide is our actual internal forecast at the time we report and we strive for accuracy, not conservatism. Our primary financial metrics are revenue for growth and operating margin for profitability. Our goals are to sustain healthy revenue growth, expand our operating margin and grow free cash flow.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">For Q4&#8217;24, we forecast 15% revenue growth, or 17% on a F&#47;X neutral basis. We expect paid net additions to be higher in Q4 than in Q3&#8217;24 due to normal seasonality and a strong content slate. We project Q4 operating margin of 22%, a five percentage point year-over-year improvement. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Our fourth quarter guidance implies that revenue will grow 15% year over year for the full year 2024, at the high end of our prior 14%-15% revenue growth expectation. Given the slightly higher revenue forecast, we&#8217;re now forecasting 2024 operating margin of 27% based on F&#47;X rates as of 1&#47;1&#47;24 and on a reported basis, up from 26% previously. This would represent a six percentage point increase compared with the full year 2023.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">We&#8217;re pleased that we&#8217;ve reaccelerated our growth and, as we head into 2025, we expect to deliver solid revenue and profit growth by both improving our core series and film offering while investing in new growth initiatives like ads and gaming. For 2025, based on F&#47;X rates as of 9&#47;30&#47;24, we forecast </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:2pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">__________________________________</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">1 </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Excluding the year over year effect of foreign exchange rate movements and the impact of hedging gains&#47;losses realized as revenues. Assumes foreign exchange rates remained constant with foreign exchange rates from each of the corresponding months of the prior-year period.</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">2 </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">ARM (Average Revenue per Membership) is defined as streaming revenue divided by the average number of streaming paid memberships divided by the number of months in the period. These figures do not include sales taxes or VAT.</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:5.2pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-2.8pt;vertical-align:baseline">3</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> Similar to recent quarters, the primary difference between F&#47;X neutral and reported growth for both revenue and ARM was large peso price increases in Argentina due to local inflation and the devaluation of the Argentine peso relative to the US dollar.</font></div><div style="height:63pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><table style="border-collapse:collapse;display:inline-table;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:100.000%"><tr><td style="width:1.0%"></td><td style="width:25.182%"></td><td style="width:0.1%"></td><td style="width:1.0%"></td><td style="width:72.618%"></td><td style="width:0.1%"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="3" style="padding:0 1pt"><div><img alt="nflxlogo2015a22a.jpg" src="nflxlogo2015a22a.jpg" style="height:22px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:86px"></div></td><td colspan="3" style="padding:2px 1pt;text-align:left;vertical-align:top"><div style="text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">2</font></div></td></tr></table></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:63pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">revenue of $43B-$44B, which would represent growth of 11%-13% off of our 2024 revenue guidance of $38.9B. We expect revenue growth to be driven by a healthy increase in paid memberships and ARM. We&#8217;re targeting a 2025 operating margin of 28% (also based on F&#47;X rates as of 9&#47;30) vs. our forecast for 27% in 2024&#59; after delivering outsized margin improvement in 2024, we want to balance near term margin growth with investing appropriately in our business. We still see plenty of room to increase our margins over the long term.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Engagement &#38; Content</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Our members rely on Netflix to entertain them, and we want to be the first place they go for that entertainment. With an audience of 600M+ and growing, we&#8217;re programming for more tastes, cultures and languages than any company has ever done before. It&#8217;s why we invest in a wide variety of TV shows and films, and work so hard to make them great. Because when people love something, they&#8217;ll keep coming back (increased retention), talk more about Netflix (increased acquisition) and place a higher value on our service. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">A strong measure of whether members loved a title is watch time. How many people liked a movie or TV show enough to press play and stay&#63; It&#8217;s why we share </font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">Weekly Top 10 lists</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">4</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> and twice a year </font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">engagement reports</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">5</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">, both of which are based on views (i.e. the total hours watched divided by the run time) and demonstrate that success on Netflix comes in all shapes and sizes. We have mega hits with enormous audiences, and hugely successful shows or movies with smaller ones. Critical acclaim is another measure of success that&#8217;s especially important for our creators. At this year&#8217;s Primetime Emmys, our talent received </font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;text-decoration:underline">107 nominations and 24 wins</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">6</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> across multiple genres &#8212; from </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Ripley</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> and </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">The Crown</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> to </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Beckham</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">, </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Blue Eye Samurai</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> and </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Love on the Spectrum</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Baby Reindeer</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> took home six awards, including Outstanding Limited Series, best actor and writing for creator Richard Gadd and best supporting actress for Jessica Gunning. All in, Netflix nominated titles generated more Nielsen Top 10 view hours, and appeared on these lists more frequently, than all other streamers combined.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Engagement on Netflix is healthy&#58; around two hours a day per paid membership on average, despite the impact of paid sharing. As we&#8217;ve discussed before, paid sharing led to lower viewing on accounts that were shared as fewer people were watching on them. In addition, when sharers bought their own subscriptions, much of that viewing was already reflected in hours viewed (impacting the trend in view hours per membership). When you isolate owner households (which excludes the impact of paid sharing), view hours for those owner households rose year over year in the first three quarters of 2024.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Programming for such a large, engaged audience, with so much variety and great quality, is hard. Netflix is already an extraordinary package of series and films (licensed and original), and increasingly games and live events &#8212; all in one place and for one price, easy to use and great value for money. At just under 10% of TV time today in our biggest countries, we believe there&#8217;s a huge opportunity to grow that share by investing even more in our slate and continuing to improve the variety and quality of our offering. Part of that improvement is ensuring we have a steady drumbeat of great, new TV shows, movies and games throughout the year to satisfy our members.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Our 2024 programming has been patchier than normal due to last year&#8217;s strikes. Key is ensuring that we have a range of prices and plans to meet a variety of needs. Earlier this month, we increased prices in a few countries in EMEA plus Japan and starting tomorrow we'll increase prices in Spain and Italy. style="text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:100%">4</font></div></td></tr></table></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:63pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">We&#8217;re now approaching the second anniversary of the launch of our advertising business and we&#8217;re making good progress. Our ads plan allows us to offer a lower price point for consumers, which is proving to be popular&#58; in Q3, it accounted for over 50% of sign-ups in our ads countries and membership on our ads plan grew 35% quarter over quarter. We&#8217;re on track to reach what we believe to be critical ad subscriber scale for advertisers in all of our ads countries in 2025, creating a strong base from which we can further increase our ad membership in 2026 and beyond. We&#8217;re also pleased with the engagement on our ads plan with view hours per membership similar to engagement on our standard plan in our 12 ads countries. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">However, we have much more work to do improving our offering for advertisers, which will be a priority over the next few years. Our in-house first party ad tech platform is on track to roll out in Canada next month, with a broader launch to all ads countries in 2025. We&#8217;ve also expanded our programmatic capabilities with The Trade Desk and Google DV 360, which is going well. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">It&#8217;s still very early for our advertising initiative. As we said last quarter, it takes time to build a new revenue stream and we don&#8217;t expect ads to be a primary driver of our revenue growth in 2025. The near term challenge (and medium term opportunity) is that we&#8217;re scaling faster than our ability to monetize our growing ad inventory. While this creates a short term drag on ARM, we are balancing building ads scale (for more meaningful ads revenue and ARM contribution over time) while still delivering healthy overall revenue growth in the near term (as noted, we expect our total company revenue to grow 15% year over year in 2024). And we&#8217;re making progress with ads monetization, as we saw in this year&#8217;s US Upfront - closing deals with all major holding companies as well as independent agencies, with a 150% plus increase in upfront ad sales commitments over 2023, in-line with our expectations.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Cash Flow and Capital Structure</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Net cash generated by operating activities in Q3 was $2.3B vs. $2.0B in the prior year period. Free cash flow (FCF)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">15</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> totaled $2.2B compared with $1.9B in last year&#8217;s Q3.  For the full year, we now expect 2024 FCF of $6.0B-$6.5B (assuming no material swings in F&#47;X rates), up from approximately $6B due to our higher operating income forecast. During Q3, we repurchased 2.6M shares for $1.7B, and we have $3.1B remaining under our existing authorization. We also raised $1.8B in our first investment grade bond deal during Q3. As a result, our total debt increased to $16B from $14B in Q2, but net debt</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">16</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> decreased from $7.4B in Q2 to $6.8B at the end of Q3. Proceeds from our bond offering will be used to pay down $1.8B in bonds that mature over the next 12 months. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:111%">Reference</font></div><div><font style="color:#666666;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Use of Non-GAAP Measures</font></div><div><font style="color:#222222;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">This shareholder letter and its attachments include reference to the non-GAAP financial measures of F&#47;X neutral revenue and adjusted operating profit and margin, free cash flow and net debt. Management believes that free cash flow is an important liquidity metric because it measures, during a given period, the amount of cash generated that is available to repay debt obligations, make strategic acquisitions and investments and for certain other activities like stock repurchases. Management believes that F&#47;X neutral revenue and adjusted operating profit and margin allow investors to compare our projected results to our actual results absent year-over-year and intra-year currency fluctuations, respectively, and the impact of restructuring costs. Management believes net debt is a useful measure of the company's liquidity, capital structure, and leverage. However, these non-GAAP financial measures should be considered in addition to, not as a substitute for or superior to, net income, operating income (profit), operating margin, diluted earnings per share and net cash provided by (used in) operating activities, or other financial measures prepared in accordance with GAAP. Reconciliation to the GAAP equivalent of these non-GAAP measures are contained in tabular form on the attached unaudited financial statements and in the F&#47;X neutral operating margin disclosure above. We are not able to reconcile forward-looking non-GAAP financial measures because we are unable to predict without unreasonable effort the exact amount or timing of the reconciling items, including property and equipment and change in other assets, and the impact of changes in currency exchange rates. The variability of these items could have a significant impact on our future GAAP financial results.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#666666;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Forward-Looking Statements</font></div><div><font style="color:#222222;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">This shareholder letter contains certain forward-looking statements within the meaning of the federal securities laws, including statements regarding our expected results for the fiscal quarter and fiscal year ending December 31, 2024&#59; adoption and growth of streaming entertainment&#59; growth strategy and outlook&#59; market opportunity&#59; competitive landscape and position&#59; entertainment offerings, including TV shows, movies, games, and live programming&#59; engagement&#59; slate strength&#59; pricing and plans strategy&#59; ad-supported tier and its prospects&#59; advertising business, including the launch of our ad-tech platform&#59; product strategy&#59; partnerships&#59; impact of foreign exchange rates&#59; foreign currency exchange hedging program&#59;  stock repurchases&#59; debt refinancings and expected use of proceeds&#59; paid net additions&#59; revenue and revenue growth&#59; ARM, operating income, operating margin, net income, earnings per share, and free cash flow.
